## Callbacks

These functions are called by the engine automatically:

| Callback | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `luna.load()` | Called once after the script is loaded |
| `luna.update(dt)` | Called every frame; `dt` is elapsed seconds |
| `luna.draw()` | Called every frame for rendering |
| `luna.keypressed(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is pressed |
| `luna.keyreleased(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is released |
| `luna.mousepressed(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is pressed |
| `luna.mousereleased(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is released |
| `luna.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch start |
| `luna.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch move |
| `luna.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch end |
| `luna.resize(w, h)` | Called when window is resized |
| `luna.focus(focused)` | Called when window gains/loses focus |
| `luna.quit()` | Called when the window is closed |
| `luna.gamepadpressed(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button press |
| `luna.gamepadreleased(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button release |
| `luna.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)` | Called on gamepad axis change |

#### `luna.graphics.arc`

Draws a filled or outlined arc segment centered at (x, y) with the given radius.

**Parameters:**

- `mode` ÔÇö Draw mode: 'fill' or 'line'.
- `x` ÔÇö Center X coordinate in pixels.
- `y` ÔÇö Center Y coordinate in pixels.
- `radius` ÔÇö Arc radius in pixels.
- `angle1` ÔÇö Start angle in radians.
- `angle2` ÔÇö End angle in radians.
- `segments` ÔÇö Optional number of line segments for smoothness.
Draws an arc.
Lua API: luna.graphics.arc(mode, x, y, radius, angle1, angle2, segments?)

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L3817)*

---

#### `luna.graphics.captureScreenshot(callback)`

Captures the current frame as an `ImageData` and passes it to `callback`.

In headless or test mode this creates a blank transparent `ImageData` sized to the current window dimensions and calls `callback` synchronously (GPU pixel readback is deferred to future full-GPU implementation). Setting `pending_screenshot` in `SharedState` allows engine-side code to detect that a capture was requested.

**Parameters:**

- `callback` — `function`. Called with one `ImageData` argument.

**Returns:** Nothing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L4407)*

---

#### `luna.graphics.circle(mode, x, y, r)`

Draws a filled or outlined circle centered at (x, y) with the given radius.

**Parameters:**

- `mode` ÔÇö Draw mode: 'fill' or 'line'.
- `x` ÔÇö Center X coordinate in pixels.
- `y` ÔÇö Center Y coordinate in pixels.
- `radius` ÔÇö Circle radius in pixels.
- `segments` ÔÇö Optional number of line segments (default auto).
Draws a circle.
Lua API: luna.graphics.circle(mode, x, y, r)

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L2922)*

#### `luna.graphics.draw(args)`

Queues draw commands for all live particles.

Lua API: luna.graphics.draw(image_id, x, y) Draws any drawable object — Image, Canvas, or SpriteBatch — at the given position. Backward-compatible: still accepts raw integer image IDs.

**Parameters:**

- `drawable` — `Drawable`. An Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata, or integer image ID.
- `x` — `f32`. Destination X position (default 0).
- `y` — `f32`. Destination Y position (default 0).
- `r` — `f32`. Rotation in radians (default 0).
- `sx` — `f32`. X scale (default 1).
- `sy` — `f32`. Y scale (default 1).
- `ox` — `f32`. X origin offset (default 0).
- `oy` — `f32`. Y origin offset (default 0).

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L3124)*

---

#### `luna.graphics.drawBatch(batch_val)`

Draws all sprites in a SpriteBatch using a single efficient GPU draw call.

**Parameters:**

- `batch` ÔÇö SpriteBatch ID returned by newSpriteBatch.
- `x` ÔÇö Optional X offset in pixels.
- `y` ÔÇö Optional Y offset in pixels.
Luna graphics API function.
Lua API: luna.graphics.drawBatch(batch_id)

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L1264)*

#### `luna.graphics.drawEx(args)`

Draws any drawable object with a full affine transform.

Accepts Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata or raw integer image IDs. When `sy` is omitted it defaults to `sx` for uniform scaling.

**Parameters:**

- `drawable` — `Drawable`. An Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch userdata or integer image ID.
- `x` — `f32`. Destination X position.
- `y` — `f32`. Destination Y position.
- `r` — `f32`. Rotation in radians (default 0).
- `sx` — `f32`. X scale (default 1).
- `sy` — `f32`. Y scale (default sx).
- `ox` — `f32`. X origin offset (default 0).
- `oy` — `f32`. Y origin offset (default 0).

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs](src/lua_api/graphics_api.rs#L3908)*

---

## luna.window

Window Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for window api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*45 entries | 45 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.window.close()`

Requests the application to close the window.

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L386)*

---

#### `luna.window.focus()`

Requests the window manager to bring the window to the foreground.

On most desktop platforms this simply raises the window.  On some compositors the OS may choose to flash the taskbar entry instead of actually raising.

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L523)*

---

#### `luna.window.fromPixels(value)`

Converts physical pixels to device-independent coordinates.

@param value : number @return any

**Parameters:** `value`

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L300)*

---

#### `luna.window.getDPIScale()`

Returns the DPI scaling factor for the window.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L279)*

---

#### `luna.window.getDesktopDimensions()`

Returns the desktop resolution (width, height) for the given display.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L260)*

---

#### `luna.window.getDimensions()`

Returns the window dimensions (width, height).

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L74)*

---

#### `luna.window.getDisplayCount()`

## luna.input

Input Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for input api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

### Transform Methods

#### `Transform:clone()`

Returns an independent deep copy of this transform object.

**Returns:** A new Transform with identical matrix state.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L218)*

---

#### `Transform:getMatrix()`

Returns the 16 matrix elements of the 4x4 transform in column-major order.

**Returns:** 16 numbers representing the matrix elements.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L230)*

---

#### `Transform:inverse()`

Returns a new Transform that is the mathematical inverse of this one.

**Returns:** A new Transform whose matrix is the inverse.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L206)*

---

#### `Transform:inverseTransformPoint(x, y)`

Applies the inverse of this transform to the given point.

**Parameters:**

- `x` — Input X coordinate.
- `y` — Input Y coordinate.

**Returns:** Inverse-transformed x, y coordinates.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L197)*

---

#### `Transform:reset()`

Resets the internal matrix to the identity (no transform applied).

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L140)*

---

#### `Transform:rotate(angle)`

Applies a rotation by the given angle to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `angle` — Rotation angle in radians.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L113)*

---

#### `Transform:scale(sx, [sy])`

Applies a scale factor to the transform's internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `sx` — Horizontal scale factor.
- `sy` — Vertical scale factor (defaults to sx if omitted).

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L123)*

---

#### `Transform:shear(kx, ky)`

Applies a shear (skew) transformation to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `kx` — Horizontal shear factor.
- `ky` — Vertical shear factor.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L134)*

---

#### `Transform:transformPoint(x, y)`

Transforms a point (x, y) by this matrix and returns the result.

**Parameters:**

- `x` — Input X coordinate.
- `y` — Input Y coordinate.

**Returns:** Transformed x, y coordinates.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L184)*

---

#### `Transform:translate(dx, dy)`

Applies a translation offset to the internal matrix.

**Parameters:**

- `dx` — Horizontal offset in pixels.
- `dy` — Vertical offset in pixels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/math_api.rs](src/lua_api/math_api.rs#L104)*

## luna.audio

Audio Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for audio api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaSource`, `LuaBus`, `LuaMidiPlayer`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*159 entries | 159 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.audio.clearFilter(id_val)`

Removes any active filter from the audio source.

@param id_val : any

**Parameters:** `id_val`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1872)*

---

#### `luna.audio.clearMidiSoundFont()`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L2027)*

---

- `buffersize` — Optional number of samples per chunk (default 2048).

@param buffersize : number?
@return any

---

#### `luna.audio.newQueueableSource`

Creates a queueable audio source that accepts manually-pushed PCM buffers.

**Parameters:**

- `sample_rate` — `u32`. Sample rate in Hz (e.g. 44100).
- `bit_depth` — `u8`. Bit depth (8 or 16).
- `channels` — `u8`. Channel count (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).
- `buffer_count` — `usize?`. Max queued buffer slots (default 4).

**Returns:** Queueable source ID (integer).
@param sample_rate : integer
@param bit_depth : integer
@param channels : integer
@param buffer_count : integer?
@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L2082)*

---

#### `luna.audio.newSoundData(args)`

Creates a raw PCM audio buffer for building procedurally generated sound.

**Parameters:**

- `samples` — Total number of PCM samples to allocate.
- `sampleRate` — Sample rate in Hz (e.g. 44100).
- `bitDepth` — Bit depth per sample (8 or 16).
- `channels` — Number of channels (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).

**Returns:** New SoundData object ID.
@param args : MultiValue

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1924)*

---

#### `luna.audio.newSource(args)`

Loads an audio file and returns a source handle.

@param args : MultiValue @return any

**Parameters:** `args`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1066)*

---

#### `Bus:getVolume()`

Returns the current volume scale of this audio mixer bus.

@return any

**Returns:** Volume scale in the range 0.0 (silent) to 1.0 (full volume).

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L369)*

---

#### `Bus:isPaused()`

Returns whether this bus is currently paused.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L411)*

---

#### `Bus:pause()`

Pauses all audio sources that are currently playing through this bus.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L392)*

---

#### `Bus:resume()`

Resumes all paused sources on this bus.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L401)*

---

#### `Bus:setPitch(pitch)`

Sets the pitch multiplier for all sources on this bus.

**Parameters:** `pitch`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L376)*

---

@param vol : number

**Parameters:** `vol`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L356)*

### Decoder Methods

#### `Decoder:getBitDepth()`

---

#### `Decoder:getChannelCount()`

Return the number of audio channels.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L990)*

---

#### `Decoder:getDuration()`

Return the total duration in seconds.

**Returns:** `f64`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1012)*

---

#### `Decoder:getSampleRate()`

Return the sample rate in Hz.

**Returns:** `u32`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1006)*

---

#### `Decoder:isSeekable()`

Returns whether this decoder supports seeking.

**Returns:** `boolean` — always `true` for in-memory decoders.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1041)*

---

#### `Decoder:release()`

Release the decoder (no-op in the current model).

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1044)*

---

#### `Decoder:rewind()`

Rewind to the beginning.

### MidiPlayer Methods

#### `MidiPlayer:getBus()`

Returns the audio bus that this MIDI player's output is routed through.

@return any

**Returns:** Bus object, or nil if no bus is assigned.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L612)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getChannelCount()`

Returns the number of MIDI channels present in the loaded sequence.

@return any

**Returns:** Channel count as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L781)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getChannelInstrument(ch)`

Returns the General MIDI instrument index for the given MIDI channel.

@param ch : integer @return any

**Parameters:**

- `channel` — 1-based MIDI channel number (1-16).

**Returns:** GM instrument index (0-127).

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L768)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getChannelVolume(ch)`

Returns the current volume scale applied to the given MIDI channel.

@param ch : integer @return any

**Parameters:**

- `channel` — 1-based MIDI channel number (1-16).

**Returns:** Volume scale in [0.0, 1.0].

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L710)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getDuration()`

Returns the total duration of the audio source in seconds.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L558)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getFilePath()`

Returns the file path of the MIDI file currently loaded into the player.

@return any

**Returns:** Path string, or nil if no file is loaded.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L480)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getNoteCount()`

Returns the total number of note events in the loaded MIDI sequence.

@return any

**Returns:** Note count as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L871)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getOriginalTempo()`

Returns the original tempo written in the MIDI file, in beats per minute.

@return any

**Returns:** Tempo in BPM.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L654)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getSoundFontPath()`

Returns the file path of the SoundFont (.sf2) currently loaded into the player.

@return any

**Returns:** Path string, or nil if using built-in defaults.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L500)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getTempo()`

Returns the current playback tempo in beats per minute.

@return any

**Returns:** Tempo as a number in BPM.

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L644)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getTempoScale()`

@return any

**Returns:** Tempo scale as a number (1.0 = original tempo).

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L673)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:getVolume()`

- `channel` — 1-based MIDI channel number (1-16).

#### `MidiPlayer:isLoaded()`

---

#### `MidiPlayer:isLooping()`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L571)*

---

#### `MidiPlayer:isPaused()`

## luna.physics

Registers the `luna.physics.*` physics API.

*108 entries | 108 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.physics.addDistanceJoint`

Adds a distance joint that maintains a fixed separation between two body anchor points.

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID.
- `body2` ÔÇö Second body ID.
- `x1`, `y1` ÔÇö Anchor on body1 in local coordinates.
- `x2`, `y2` ÔÇö Anchor on body2 in local coordinates.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L2501)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addFrictionJoint`

Adds a friction joint that resists relative movement and rotation between two bodies.

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID.
- `body2` ÔÇö Second body ID.
- `ax`, `ay` ÔÇö World-space anchor point.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L854)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addGearJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, ax, ay)`

Adds a gear joint that couples two revolute or prismatic joints so they move in sync.

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `joint1` ÔÇö First revolute or prismatic joint ID.
- `joint2` ÔÇö Second revolute or prismatic joint ID.
- `ratio` ÔÇö Gear ratio between the two joints.

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L995)*

---

#### `luna.physics.addMotorJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, cf)`

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID (reference).
- `body2` ÔÇö Second body ID (driven).

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L890)*

---

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body` ÔÇö Body ID to control.
- `x`, `y` ÔÇö Initial target position in world coordinates.

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID.
- `body2` ÔÇö Second body ID.
- `ax`, `ay` ÔÇö World-space anchor point.

---

#### `luna.physics.addPulleyJoint(world_id_val, body_a, body_b, ax, ay)`

Adds a pulley joint linking two bodies through a rope of fixed total length.

**Parameters:**

- `world` ÔÇö World ID.
- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID.
- `body2` ÔÇö Second body ID.
- `gx1`, `gy1` ÔÇö Ground anchor for body1 in world coordinates.
- `gx2`, `gy2` ÔÇö Ground anchor for body2 in world coordinates.
- `ax1`, `ay1` ÔÇö Body1 attachment point in local coordinates.
- `ax2`, `ay2` ÔÇö Body2 attachment point in local coordinates.
- `ratio` ÔÇö Pulley ratio (1.0 = symmetric).

**Returns:** New joint ID.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L969)*

---

- `body1` ÔÇö First body ID.

#### `luna.physics.attachShape(body_ud, shape_ud)`

- `x1` ÔÇö Ray origin X in world units.
- `y1` ÔÇö Ray origin Y in world units.
- `x2` ÔÇö Ray end X in world units.
- `y2` ÔÇö Ray end Y in world units.

- `world` ÔÇö World ID to cast in.
- `x1` ÔÇö Ray origin X in world units.
- `y1` ÔÇö Ray origin Y in world units.
- `x2` ÔÇö Ray end X in world units.
- `y2` ÔÇö Ray end Y in world units.

**Returns:** Table of {body, x, y, nx, ny, fraction} hit records ordered by fraction.

### Body Methods

#### `Body:addFixture(params)`

Adds a collision fixture to the body using the given shape definition table.

**Parameters:**

- `def` ÔÇö Table describing the fixture: shape, density, friction, restitution.

**Returns:** Fixture ID for the newly attached fixture.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L505)*

---

#### `Body:applyForce(fx, fy)`

Applies a continuous force (accumulates until the next physics step) to the body's centre of mass.

**Parameters:**

- `fx` ÔÇö `number`: Horizontal force component.
- `fy` ÔÇö `number`: Vertical force component.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L457)*

---

#### `Body:applyImpulse(ix, iy)`

Applies an instantaneous impulse directly to the body's centre of mass.

**Parameters:**

- `ix` ÔÇö `number`: Horizontal impulse.
- `iy` ÔÇö `number`: Vertical impulse.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L470)*

---

#### `Body:destroy()`

Destroys the body and removes it from its parent physics world immediately.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L488)*

---

#### `Body:getAngle()`

Returns the body's current rotation angle in radians.

**Returns:** `number` ÔÇö angle in radians.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L404)*

---

#### `Body:getBodyType()`

Returns the type string of the given body.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L479)*

---

#### `Body:getFixtureCount()`

Returns the number of collision fixtures currently attached to the body.

**Returns:** Fixture count as an integer.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L564)*

---

#### `Body:getMass()`

Returns the total simulated mass of the body in physics units.

**Returns:** Mass as a number in physics units.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L428)*

---

#### `Body:getPosition()`

Returns the body's current world-space position.

**Returns:** Two numbers `x, y` in world units.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L348)*

---

#### `Body:getVelocity()`

Returns the current linear velocity vector of the body.

**Returns:** vx, vy velocity in world units per second.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L375)*

---

#### `Body:setAngle(angle)`

Sets the body's rotation to `angle` radians (bypasses physics).

**Parameters:**

- `angle` ÔÇö `number`: Target angle in radians.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L416)*

---

#### `Body:setPosition(x, y)`

Teleports the body to the given world-space position (bypasses collision detection).

**Parameters:**

- `x` ÔÇö `number`: Target X position.
- `y` ÔÇö `number`: Target Y position.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L363)*

---

#### `Body:setSize(w, h)`

Resizes the body's primary collision shape to the given width and height.

**Parameters:**

- `width` ÔÇö New shape width in world units.
- `height` ÔÇö New shape height in world units.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L441)*

---

#### `Body:setVelocity(vx, vy)`

Sets the body's linear velocity to the given (vx, vy) world-space vector.

**Parameters:**

- `vx` ÔÇö Velocity along the X axis in world units per second.
- `vy` ÔÇö Velocity along the Y axis in world units per second.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L390)*

---

### Shape Methods

#### `Shape:destroy()`

Destroys the shape. No-op — Lua GC handles cleanup automatically.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L92)*

---

#### `Shape:getBoundingBox()`

Returns the axis-aligned bounding box of this shape in local coordinates.

**Returns:** Four numbers `x1, y1, x2, y2` (min corner, max corner).

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L50)*

---

#### `Shape:getRadius()`

Returns the radius of a circle shape.

**Returns:** `number` — radius; errors for non-circle shapes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L39)*

---

#### `Shape:getType()`

Returns the shape type string: `"circle"`, `"rectangle"`, `"polygon"`, `"edge"`, or `"chain"`.

**Returns:** `string`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L31)*

---

#### `Shape:setDensity(density)`

Sets the density for when this shape is attached to a body.

**Parameters:**

- `density` — `number`. Mass per unit area.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L59)*

---

#### `Shape:setFriction(friction)`

Sets the friction coefficient for when this shape is attached to a body.

**Parameters:**

- `friction` — `number`. Surface friction (0 = frictionless, 1 = high friction).

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L68)*

---

#### `Shape:setRestitution(restitution)`

Sets the restitution (bounciness) for when this shape is attached to a body.

**Parameters:**

- `restitution` — `number`. 0 = inelastic, 1 = fully elastic.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L77)*

---

#### `Shape:setSensor(sensor)`

Sets whether this shape acts as a sensor (detects overlaps, no forces).

**Parameters:**

- `sensor` — `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L86)*

---

#### `World:getCollisions()`

Returns a table of all currently active collision pairs in this physics world.

**Returns:** Table of {bodyA, bodyB, nx, ny, overlap} collision records.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L280)*

---

#### `World:getGravity()`

Returns the current world gravity vector.

**Returns:** Two numbers `gx, gy`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L222)*

---

#### `World:isSleepingAllowed(body_id)`

Returns whether bodies in this world are allowed to enter a sleep state.

**Parameters:** `body_id`

**Returns:** true if sleeping is permitted globally, false if all bodies stay awake.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L259)*

---

#### `World:setCallbacks(callbacks)`

Registers collision begin/end callback functions for this physics world.

**Parameters:**

- `beginContact` ÔÇö Called with (body1, body2) when two bodies start touching.
- `endContact` ÔÇö Called with (body1, body2) when they separate.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L206)*

---

#### `World:setGravity(gx, gy)`

Sets world gravity. Default is `(0, 9.81)` (downward).

**Parameters:**

- `x` ÔÇö `number`: Horizontal gravity component.
- `y` ÔÇö `number`: Vertical gravity component.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L236)*

---

#### `World:step(dt)`

Advances the physics simulation by `dt` seconds, resolving collisions and integrating forces.

**Parameters:**

- `dt` ÔÇö `number`: Elapsed simulation time in seconds.

*Source: [src/lua_api/physics_api.rs](src/lua_api/physics_api.rs#L141)*

---


## luna.filesystem

Filesystem Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for filesystem api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*37 entries | 37 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.filesystem.append(path, data)`

Opens the file in append mode and writes the given string at the end.

**Parameters:**

- `path` — Relative file path inside the save directory.
- `data` — String to append.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.
@param path : string
@param data : string

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L242)*

### FileHandle Methods

#### `FileHandle:close()`

Flushes any pending writes and closes the file handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L144)*

---

#### `FileHandle:flush()`

Flushes all buffered writes to disk without closing the handle.

**Returns:** true on success, or nil plus an error string on failure.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L133)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getMode()`

Returns the access mode the file was opened with.

@return any

**Returns:** One of 'r' (read), 'w' (write), or 'a' (append).

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L124)*

---

#### `FileHandle:getSize()`

Returns the size of the open file in bytes.

@return any

**Returns:** File size as an integer number of bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs](src/lua_api/filesystem_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `FileHandle:isEOF()`

- `offset` — Byte position to seek to (0-based).

## luna.event

Event Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for event api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*14 entries | 14 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.event.clear()`

Discards all pending events in the queue.

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L253)*

---

#### `luna.event.newSignal()`

Event.

Creates a new pub-sub Signal dispatcher. @return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L266)*

---

#### `luna.event.poll()`

Polls and returns the next event from the queue, or nil if empty.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L223)*

---

#### `luna.event.pump()`

Syncs OS-level events into the queue. In Luna2D this is a no-op (push model).

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L279)*

---

#### `luna.event.push(args)`

Pushes a custom event onto the event queue.

@param args : MultiValue

**Parameters:** `args`

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L180)*

---

#### `luna.event.quit([code])`

Pushes a quit event onto the event queue, requesting the engine to stop.

**Parameters:**

- `exitcode` — Optional integer exit code (default 0).
@param code : integer?

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L166)*

---

#### `luna.event.restart()`

Requests that the engine restart at the beginning of the next frame.

Sets `SharedState::restart_requested` to `true`. The engine loop checks this flag after each frame and restarts if set.

**Returns:** `()`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L330)*

---

#### `luna.event.wait([timeout])`

Blocks until the next event arrives or the optional timeout elapses.

**Parameters:**

- `timeout` — `number?`. Timeout in seconds (optional; omit to wait indefinitely).

**Returns:** Event name and arguments, or nothing on timeout.

*Source: [src/lua_api/event_api.rs](src/lua_api/event_api.rs#L296)*

---

## luna.thread

Registers the `luna.thread` namespace.

Provides Lua-level multithreading: create background threads that run
independent Lua VMs and communicate via thread-safe channels.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for thread api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaThreadHandle`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.thread.getChannel(name)`

Get or create a named global channel (singleton, shared across threads).

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L142)*

---

#### `luna.thread.newChannel()`

Create an unnamed thread-safe channel for inter-thread communication.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L127)*

---

#### `luna.thread.newThread(code)`

Create a new background thread from a Lua code string.

The thread gets its own Lua VM and can communicate via channels. @param code : string @return any

**Parameters:** `code`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L114)*

---

### ThreadHandle Methods

#### `ThreadHandle:getError()`

Returns the error message if the thread terminated with a Lua error, or `nil` if it completed normally.

@return any

**Returns:** `string` — error message, or `nil`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L82)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:isRunning()`

Returns `true` if the thread is currently executing.

@return any

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L72)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:start(args)`

Launches the background thread, passing optional arguments to the Lua script via `...`.

@param args : MultiValue

**Parameters:**

- `...` — `any`: Optional arguments forwarded to the thread script as Lua values.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L50)*

---

#### `ThreadHandle:wait()`

Blocks the calling coroutine until this thread finishes execution.

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L61)*

### AIWorld Methods

#### `AIWorld:addAgent(name)`

Registers a new agent named `name` in this world and returns its handle.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`: Unique identifier for the new agent.

**Returns:** An `Agent` handle ready for further configuration.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L182)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getAgent(name)`

Looks up a registered agent by name.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`: Name of the agent to retrieve.

**Returns:** The `Agent` handle, or `nil` if no agent with that name exists.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L200)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getAgentCount()`

Returns the number of agents currently registered in this world.

@return any

**Returns:** `integer` — total agent count.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L229)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getGlobalBlackboard()`

Returns a snapshot of the shared world-level blackboard.

@return any

**Returns:** A `Blackboard` containing data visible to all agents in this world.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L238)*

---

#### `AIWorld:removeAgent(agent)`

Removes and destroys the given agent from this world.

@param agent : Agent

**Parameters:**

- `agent` — `Agent`: Handle of the agent to remove, obtained from `addAgent`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L217)*

---

#### `AIWorld:update(dt)`

Advances all agents in the world by `dt` seconds, integrating velocity into position.

@param dt : number

**Parameters:**

- `dt` — `number`: Elapsed seconds since the last frame.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L250)*

---

---

#### `Agent:setPosition(x, y)`

Teleports the agent to world-space coordinates (`x`, `y`).

@param x : number @param y : number

**Parameters:**

- `x` — `number`: Horizontal world-space position.
- `y` — `number`: Vertical world-space position.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L279)*

---

#### `Agent:setPriority(p)`

Sets the scheduling priority; higher-priority agents are processed first during `update`.

@param p : integer

**Parameters:**

- `p` — `integer`: Priority value, higher = earlier processing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L389)*

---

#### `Agent:setVelocity(x, y)`

@param x : number @param y : number

**Parameters:**

- `x` — `number`: Horizontal component.
- `y` — `number`: Vertical component.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L308)*

## luna.data

Registers the `luna.data.*` binary data, compression, hashing, and encoding API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for data api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*21 entries | 12 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.data.compress(format_str, raw_data, [level])`

Compresses data using the given algorithm ('deflate', 'gzip', 'lz4').

@param format_str : string @param raw_data : string @param level : integer? @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `raw_data`, `level`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L57)*

---

#### `luna.data.decode(format_str, encoded)`

Decodes binary data from a buffer according to a pack-format string.

@param format_str : string @param encoded : string

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `data` — Binary string or ByteData buffer to read from.

**Returns:** Decoded Lua values followed by the next unread byte offset.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L132)*

---

#### `luna.data.decompress(format_str, compressed_data)`

Decompresses data using the given algorithm.

@param format_str : string @param compressed_data : string @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `compressed_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L76)*

---

#### `luna.data.encode(format_str, raw_data)`

Encodes Lua values into a binary string using a pack-format string.

@param format_str : string @param raw_data : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `...` — Values to encode.

**Returns:** Binary string containing the packed bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L112)*

---

#### `luna.data.encodeToml(table)`

Encodes a Lua table as a TOML string.

@param table : table

**Parameters:** `table`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L156)*

---

#### `luna.data.getPackedSize(fmt, vals)`

Returns the total byte count that pack() would produce for the given format and values.

For fixed-width types no values are needed. String types (s/z) require the values. @param format : string @return any

**Parameters:** `fmt`, `vals`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L205)*

---

#### `luna.data.hash(algo_str, raw_data)`

@param algo_str : string @param raw_data : string @return any

**Parameters:** `algo_str`, `raw_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L92)*

## luna.graph

Registers the `luna.graph.*` directed-graph and item-flow simulation API.

Exposes `LuaGraph`, `LuaNode`, `LuaEdge`, and `LuaGraphItem` UserData types
wrapping `crate::graph::Graph` with callback dispatch for simulation events.

#### `luna.tilemap.hexArea(q, r, radius)`

Returns all hex cell coordinates within a given radius of center (q, r).

**Parameters:**

- `q` ÔÇö Center q coordinate.
- `r` ÔÇö Center r coordinate.
- `radius` ÔÇö Radius in hex steps (1 = immediate ring, 2 = two rings, etc.).

**Returns:** Table of {q, r} coordinates for every cell within the radius.

*Source: [src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs](src/lua_api/tilemap_api.rs#L2279)*

## luna.automation

Automation Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

Registers the `luna.simulator.*` namespace for automated input simulation
via timed step scripts. Scripts inject synthetic input events into the
engine's event queue during playback.

## Exposed Lua API

| Function | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `luna.simulator.load(name, data)` | Load a script from a Lua step table |
| `luna.simulator.loadFromToml(name, toml_str)` | Load a script from a TOML string |
| `luna.simulator.loadFile(name, path)` | Load a script from a TOML file on disk |
| `luna.simulator.unload(name)` | Remove a loaded script by name |
| `luna.simulator.hasScript(name)` | Return `true` if a script is registered |
| `luna.simulator.getScripts()` | Return an array of all registered script names |
| `luna.simulator.start(name)` | Start playback from step zero |
| `luna.simulator.stop()` | Stop playback and reset to `Idle` |
| `luna.simulator.pause()` | Pause playback at the current position |
| `luna.simulator.resume()` | Resume from a paused position |
| `luna.simulator.update(dt)` | Advance the clock and dispatch due steps |
| `luna.simulator.isRunning()` | Return `true` if actively playing |
| `luna.simulator.isPaused()` | Return `true` if paused |
| `luna.simulator.isComplete()` | Return `true` if all steps dispatched |
| `luna.simulator.getCurrentStep()` | Return the index of the next step |
| `luna.simulator.getStepCount()` | Return the total step count |
| `luna.simulator.getCurrentScript()` | Return the active script name or `nil` |
| `luna.simulator.getElapsedTime()` | Return seconds elapsed since `start` |

## Implementation Pattern

A single `Rc<RefCell<Simulator>>` is created at registration time and
captured by all closures via Rc clone. The `SharedState` borrow is held
only long enough to push events — never across yield points.

*16 entries | 0 documented*

#### `luna.automation.getCurrentScript()`

*(undocumented)*

details for battle api-related operations and data management.

## luna.cardgame

Lua bindings for `luna.cardgame.*`.

Exposes Card, Stack, StackBuilder, StackManager, CardPool, Slot, StackHistory,
and group-analysis utilities to Lua scripts via the `luna.cardgame` namespace.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for cardgame api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaCard`, `LuaStack`, `LuaDeckBuilder`, `LuaZoneManager`, `LuaCardPool`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*212 entries | 212 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.cardgame.clearTypes()`

Clears all registered item types.

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1949)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.defineType(name, def_tbl)`

Defines a card type in the global registry.

@param name : string @param def_tbl : table

```lua luna.cardgame.defineType("fireball", { category = "spell", subtype  = "damage", rarity   = "rare", maxPerDeck = 3, stats    = { damage = 10, manaCost = 3 }, tags     = { "fire", "instant" }, meta     = { artist = "A. Smith" }, }) ```

**Parameters:** `name`, `def_tbl`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1869)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.findAtLeastNOfStat(items_tbl, stat, n)`

Finds groups where at least `n` items share the same stat integer value.

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param n : integer @return any

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `n`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2128)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.findNOfStat(items_tbl, stat, n)`

Finds groups where exactly `n` items share the same stat integer value.

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param n : integer @return any

Returns an array of `{label, score, items}` tables.

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `n`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2105)*

---

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param min_run : integer @return any

Returns an array of `{label, score, items}` tables.

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `min_run`

@param items_tbl : table @param prefix : string @return any

---

#### `luna.cardgame.newSlot(name, [cap])`

Creates a new `Slot`.

@param name : string @param cap : integer? @return any

```lua local slot = luna.cardgame.newSlot("weapon_slot", 1)  -- holds 1 item ```

**Parameters:** `name`, `cap`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2015)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.newStack(name, [cap])`

Creates a new empty stack.

@param name : string @param cap : integer? @return any

```lua local hand = luna.cardgame.newStack("hand") local deck = luna.cardgame.newStack("deck", 60)   -- capped at 60 ```

**Parameters:** `name`, `cap`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1976)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.newStackManager()`

Alias for `newEffectStack` (LIFO effect resolution stack).

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2224)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.newZoneManager()`

Creates a new `StackManager`.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1996)*

#### `Card:fireScript(event, args)`

Fires a named script hook with optional extra arguments.

@param event : string @param args : MultiValue @return any

Looks up the instance script first; if not set, looks up the type-level script in the global `_LUNA_CG_SCRIPTS[card_type][event]` table.

**Parameters:** `event`, `args`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L401)*

### DeckBuilder Methods

#### `DeckBuilder:addRequiredCategory(cat, min, [max])`

@param cat : string @param min : integer @param max : integer?

**Parameters:** `cat`, `min`, `max`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1118)*

---

@param tag : string @param min : integer

**Parameters:** `tag`, `min`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1092)*

---

#### `DeckBuilder:addWith(type_name, count, overrides)`

Adds `count` copies with per-entry overrides supplied as a table.

@param type_name : string @param count : integer @param overrides : table

The override table may have: `stats = {key=val}`, `tags = {str, ...}`, `meta = {key=val}`.

**Parameters:** `type_name`, `count`, `overrides`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L980)*

---

#### `DeckBuilder:banType(type_name)`

Marks a type as banned (must not appear).

@param type_name : string

**Parameters:** `type_name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1007)*

## luna.combat

Lua bindings for the `luna.combat.*` vehicle combat API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for combat api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaCollisionGroupSet`, `LuaChassis`, `LuaTurret`, `LuaWeapon`, `LuaProjectile`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*110 entries | 110 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.combat.newChassis(body_id, max_hp)`

Creates a new `Chassis` with the given body ID and max HP.

@param body_id : integer @param max_hp : number @return any

**Parameters:**

- `body_id` — `integer`: Physics body ID.
- `max_hp` — `number`: Maximum hit points.

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L682)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newCollisionGroupSet()`

Creates a new `CollisionGroupSet`.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L670)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newCombatWorld()`

Creates a new empty `CombatWorld`.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L723)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newProjectilePool(size, [proj_type])`

Creates a new `ProjectilePool` with the given capacity.

@param size : integer @param proj_type : string? @return any

**Parameters:**

- `size` — `integer`: Pool capacity.
- `proj_type` — `string` optional: Projectile type (default `"ballistic"`).

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L716)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newTurret(body_id, joint_id)`

@param body_id : integer @param joint_id : integer @return any

**Parameters:**

- `body_id` — `integer`: Physics body ID.
- `joint_id` — `integer`: Revolute joint ID.

## luna.crafting

Lua bindings for `luna.crafting.*`.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for crafting api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaRecipe`, `LuaRecipeRegistry`, `LuaStation`, `LuaCraftSkill`, `LuaCraftQueue`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*177 entries | 177 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.crafting.newCraftQueue([max_jobs])`

Creates a new craft queue instance.

@param max_jobs : integer? @return any

**Parameters:**

- `max_jobs` — `integer` optional.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L2044)*

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`.

#### `luna.crafting.newRecipeGroup(name)`

@param name : string @return any

### ModifierPool Methods

#### `ModifierPool:addModifier(name, weight, [effects])`

Adds a modifier to the pool. Effects are a table of `{effectName: number}` pairs.

@param name : string @param weight : number @param effects : table?

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`: Modifier name.
- `weight` — `number`: Relative selection weight (higher = more likely).
- `effects` — `table` optional: `{[effectName]: number}` effect magnitudes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1894)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:count()`

Returns the number of entries in the pool.

@return integer

**Returns:** `integer`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1933)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:getModifiers()`

Returns all modifier entries as a list of `{name, weight, effects}` tables.

@return any

**Returns:** `table` of modifier tables.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1940)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:getName()`

Returns the name of this modifier pool.

@return any

**Returns:** `string`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1883)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:getTotalWeight()`

Returns the total combined weight of all pool entries.

@return any

**Returns:** `number`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1924)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:removeModifier(name)`

Removes a modifier by name. Returns `true` if it existed.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1915)*

---

#### `ModifierPool:roll(seed)`

Rolls a random modifier using `seed` as a deterministic source.

@param seed : integer @return any

**Parameters:**

- `seed` — `integer`: Deterministic seed value.

**Returns:** `table` — `{name, weight, effects}`, or `nil` if pool is empty.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1964)*

### RecipeKnowledge Methods

#### `RecipeKnowledge:clear()`

Clears all recipe knowledge.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1684)*

#### `RecipeKnowledge:count()`

Returns the number of known recipes.

---

#### `RecipeKnowledge:discover(id, [source])`

Marks a recipe as discovered with an optional source string.

@param id : string @param source : string?

**Parameters:**

- `recipe_id` — `string`: Recipe ID to discover.
- `source` — `string` optional: Discovery source (e.g. `'scroll'`).

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1608)*

---

#### `RecipeKnowledge:forget(id)`

@param id : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe_id` — `string`: Recipe ID to forget.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

- `recipe_id` — `string`.

---

#### `RecipeKnowledge:prototype(id)`

Permanently learns a recipe via the prototype mechanic (Don't Starve pattern).

@param id : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe_id` — `string`.

**Returns:** `boolean` — `false` if already prototyped.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1697)*

---

#### `RecipeKnowledge:research(id, scrap)`

@param id : string @param scrap : number @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe_id` — `string`.
- `scrap` — `number`: Amount of scrap to spend.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1749)*

---

#### `RecipeKnowledge:setAutoDiscover(v)`

Enables or disables auto-discovery mode (all recipes always known).

@param v : boolean

**Parameters:**

- `enabled` — `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1672)*

---

**Parameters:**

- `recipe_id` — `string`.
- `cost` — `number`: Scrap / resource cost to unlock.

### RecipeRegistry Methods

#### `RecipeRegistry:add(recipe)`

Registers a recipe in this registry. Raises an error if a recipe with the same ID already exists.

@param recipe : Recipe

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: Recipe object to register.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L435)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:count()`

Returns the total number of registered recipes.

@return integer

**Returns:** `integer`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L469)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:findByIngredient(item_type)`

Returns all recipes that consume an item with the given ID as an ingredient.

@param item_type : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `item_id` — `string`: Ingredient item ID to search for.

**Returns:** `table` of `Recipe` objects.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L505)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:findByOutput(item_type)`

Returns all recipes that produce an item with the given ID.

@param item_type : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `item_id` — `string`: Output item ID to search for.

**Returns:** `table` of `Recipe` objects.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L489)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:findByTag(tag)`

Returns all recipes that carry the given tag.

@param tag : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `tag` — `string`: Tag string to match.

**Returns:** `table` of `Recipe` objects.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L521)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:forStation(station_type)`

@param station_type : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `station_type` — `string`: Station type identifier.

**Returns:** `table` of `Recipe` objects.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L536)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:get(id)`

Returns the registered recipe with the given ID, or `nil` if none exists.

@param id : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `id` — `string`: Recipe ID to look up.

**Returns:** `Recipe` or `nil`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L449)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:getAll()`

Returns all recipes in registration order as a list of `Recipe` objects.

@return any

**Returns:** `table` of `Recipe` objects.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L573)*

@param category : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `category` — `string`: Category name.

#### `RecipeRegistry:getIds()`

@return any

**Returns:** `table` of `string` IDs.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L475)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:register(recipe)`

Alias for `add`. Registers a recipe (error if duplicate ID).

@param recipe : Recipe

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L549)*

#### `RecipeRegistry:remove(id)`

Removes the recipe with the given ID from this registry.

@param id : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `id` — `string`: Recipe ID to remove.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L461)*

---

#### `RecipeRegistry:unregister(id)`

Alias for `remove`. Unregisters the recipe with the given ID.

@param id : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `id` — `string`.

**Returns:** `boolean` — `true` if it existed.

### Station Methods

#### `Station:addFuel(amount)`

Adds fuel to this station, clamped to capacity.

@param amount : number

**Parameters:**

- `amount` — `number`: Fuel to add.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L829)*

---

#### `Station:canProcess(recipe)`

Returns `true` if this station can currently process the given recipe (level and type match).

@param recipe : Recipe @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: Recipe to check against this station's type and level.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L683)*

---

#### `Station:consumeFuel(amount)`

Consumes fuel from this station. Returns `false` if insufficient fuel.

@param amount : number @return any

**Parameters:**

- `amount` — `number`: Fuel to consume.

**Returns:** `boolean` — `true` if consumed successfully.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L842)*

---

#### `Station:effectiveTime(recipe)`

Returns the effective crafting time for `recipe` after applying this station's speed multiplier.

@param recipe : Recipe @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: The recipe to evaluate.

**Returns:** `number` — effective time in seconds.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L697)*

---

#### `Station:getFuelCapacity()`

- `from_id` — `string`.
- `to_id` — `string`.

#### `UpgradeTree:unlock(id)`

## luna.debug

Registers the `luna.devtools.*` runtime diagnostics and developer tools API.

Five subsystems: structured logger, hierarchical profiler, frame statistics,
file watcher, and Lua debug bridge. All module-level functions — no
registered types.

*33 entries | 33 documented*

## luna.debugbridge

Registers the `luna.debugbridge.*` TCP debug server API.

Embeds a JSON-over-TCP server (127.0.0.1 only) inside the running game.
External tools (VS Code extension, MCP server) connect to inspect and
control the game at runtime. Network I/O runs on a background thread;
Lua-dependent methods are queued and dispatched via `poll()` on the main thread.

*15 entries | 15 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debugbridge.broadcast(event, json_data)`

Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.

@param event : string @param json_data : string

**Parameters:** `event`, `json_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L794)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.capturePrint(msg, [source], [line])`

@param msg : string @param source : string? @param line : integer?

**Parameters:** `msg`, `source`, `line`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L620)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory()`

Clears the print history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L689)*

## luna.economy

Lua API bindings for the `luna.economy.*` named resource economy module.

Provides `ResourceManager` UserData for managing named resources with
capacity, flow rates, decay, interest, conversions, and overflow policies.

*47 entries | 47 documented*

## luna.entity

Registers the `luna.entity.*` ECS universe API.

Exposes `Universe` as Lua UserData (`LuaUniverse`) with entity lifecycle,
component operations, querying, systems, tags, layers, and blueprints.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for entity api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*40 entries | 40 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.entity.newUniverse()`

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/entity_api.rs](src/lua_api/entity_api.rs#L611)*

## luna.font

Lua API bindings for the `luna.font.*` font rasterizer module.

Provides `newRasterizer`, `newTrueTypeRasterizer`, `newBMFontRasterizer`,
and `newGlyphData` factory functions matching the LÖVE2D `love.font` module
surface.  Font loading delegates to the same `Font::from_bytes` path used by
`luna.graphics.newFont` so the returned `LuaFont` userdata is fully
compatible with all existing graphics API functions.

*11 entries | 11 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.font.newBMFontRasterizer(image_file, glyph_hints)`

Stub: BMFont rasterization is not yet supported.

Raises a descriptive Lua error so scripts fail fast with a clear message rather than a cryptic nil-dereference.

**Parameters:** `image_file`, `glyph_hints`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L199)*

---

#### `luna.font.newGlyphData(font_val, codepoint)`

Returns glyph metrics for a given Unicode code point within the font.

`font` may be a `LuaFont` userdata or a raw font ID integer. `codepoint` is a Unicode integer (e.g. `string.byte("A")` = 65).

**Parameters:** `font_val`, `codepoint`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L216)*

---

#### `luna.font.newRasterizer(path, [size])`

Loads a TTF/OTF font file and returns a font userdata object.

This is an alias for `luna.graphics.newFont` exposed on the `luna.font` module for LÖVE2D compatibility.

**Parameters:** `path`, `size`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L172)*

---

#### `luna.font.newTrueTypeRasterizer(path, [size], [hinting])`

Loads a TTF/OTF font with an optional hinting hint (currently ignored).

The `hinting` parameter is accepted for API compatibility but has no effect — fontdue uses its own hinting strategy internally.

**Parameters:** `path`, `size`, `hinting`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L185)*

---

### GlyphData Methods

#### `GlyphData:getAdvance()`

Returns the horizontal advance width in pixels.

**Returns:** `number`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L78)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getBearingX()`

Returns the horizontal bearing (cursor-to-glyph-edge offset).

**Returns:** `number`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L84)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getBearingY()`

Returns the vertical bearing (baseline-to-glyph-top offset).

**Returns:** `number`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L90)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getGlyph()`

Returns the Unicode code point as an integer.

**Returns:** `integer`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L96)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getGlyphString()`

Returns the glyph character as a UTF-8 string.

**Returns:** `string`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L102)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getHeight()`

Returns the pixel height of the glyph bitmap.

**Returns:** `integer`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L72)*

---

#### `GlyphData:getWidth()`

Returns the pixel width of the glyph bitmap.

**Returns:** `integer`

*Source: [src/lua_api/font_api.rs](src/lua_api/font_api.rs#L66)*

---


## luna.gui

Lua API bindings for the `luna.gui.*` retained-mode widget system.

Registers the `luna.gui` namespace with functions for creating widgets,
managing the widget tree, routing input events, theming, focus navigation,
and toast notifications.

## Exposed Lua API

| Function | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `luna.gui.newButton(text?)` | Create a button widget |
| `luna.gui.newLabel(text?)` | Create a text label |
| `luna.gui.newTextInput()` | Create a text input field |
| `luna.gui.newCheckbox(text?)` | Create a checkbox |
| `luna.gui.newSlider(min?, max?)` | Create a value slider |
| `luna.gui.newProgressBar(min?, max?)` | Create a progress bar |
| `luna.gui.newComboBox()` | Create a dropdown |
| `luna.gui.newList()` | Create a selectable list |
| `luna.gui.newPanel()` | Create a container panel |
| `luna.gui.newLayout(direction?)` | Create a flexbox layout |
| `luna.gui.newScrollPanel()` | Create a scrollable panel |
| `luna.gui.newNinePatch()` | Create a 9-patch slicer |
| `luna.gui.newTabBar()` | Create a tab bar |
| `luna.gui.newSeparator(vertical?)` | Create a separator line |
| `luna.gui.newSpacer(w?, h?)` | Create spacing filler |
| `luna.gui.newToast(msg?, duration?)` | Create a toast notification |
| `luna.gui.newTreeView()` | Create a collapsible tree |
| `luna.gui.newRadioButton(text?, group?)` | Create a grouped radio button |
| `luna.gui.newScrollBar(vertical?)` | Create a scroll bar |
| `luna.gui.newWindow(title?)` | Create a draggable window |
| `luna.gui.newSplitPanel(orientation?)` | Create a split panel |
| `luna.gui.newDockPanel()` | Create a dock panel |
| `luna.gui.newToolbar(orientation?)` | Create a toolbar |
| `luna.gui.newMenuBar()` | Create a menu bar |
| `luna.gui.newMenuItem(text?)` | Create a menu item |
| `luna.gui.newDialog(title?)` | Create a modal dialog |
| `luna.gui.newStatusBar()` | Create a status bar |
| `luna.gui.newAccordion()` | Create a collapsible accordion |
| `luna.gui.newTooltipPanel(text?)` | Create a tooltip panel |
| `luna.gui.newColorPicker()` | Create a color picker |
| `luna.gui.newTable()` | Create a data table |
| `luna.gui.newImageWidget()` | Create an image widget |
| `luna.gui.newTheme()` | Create a theme instance |
| `luna.gui.setTheme(theme)` | Set the active theme |
| `luna.gui.getTheme()` | Get the active theme |
| `luna.gui.getRoot()` | Get the root panel index |
| `luna.gui.setFocus(idx/nil)` | Set keyboard focus |
| `luna.gui.getFocus()` | Get focused widget index |
| `luna.gui.focusNext()` | Tab to next focusable |
| `luna.gui.focusPrev()` | Tab to previous focusable |
| `luna.gui.clearFocus()` | Clear focus |
| `luna.gui.addToast(toast)` | Queue a toast overlay |
| `luna.gui.getToastCount()` | Active toast count |
| `luna.gui.mousepressed(x,y,btn?)` | Forward mouse press |
| `luna.gui.mousereleased(x,y,btn?)` | Forward mouse release |
| `luna.gui.mousemoved(x,y)` | Forward mouse move |
| `luna.gui.keypressed(key)` | Forward key press |
| `luna.gui.textinput(text)` | Forward text input |
| `luna.gui.wheelmoved(x,y)` | Forward mouse wheel |
| `luna.gui.update(dt)` | Advance toast timers |
| `luna.gui.getWidgetCount()` | Total widget count |
| Widget methods | See per-type method tables in gui.md |

## Implementation Pattern

A single `Rc<RefCell<GuiContext>>` is created at registration time and
captured by all closures via Rc clone.  Widget indices (pool positions)
are returned to Lua as integers.  Container/list/tab indices are 1-based
in Lua.

*287 entries | 0 documented*

## luna.inventory

Lua API bindings for the `luna.inventory.*` slot-based inventory module.

Provides `Item`, `ItemStack`, `Slot`, `Container`, `ItemSet`, and `Inventory`
UserData objects for building RPG-style inventory systems in Lua.

*84 entries | 84 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.inventory.newContainer(name, [mode_str], [slot_count])`

New container.

@param name : string @param mode_str : string? @param slot_count : integer? @return any

**Parameters:** `name`, `mode_str`, `slot_count`

*Source: [src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs](src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs#L1438)*

*Source: [src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs](src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs#L1456)*

## luna.localization

Registers the `luna.localization.*` internationalization API.

Provides a structured translation system supporting multiple languages,
fallback chains, pluralization, variable interpolation, and language-change
callbacks.

## luna.log

Structured game-level logging API (`luna.log.*`).

Exposes convenience logging functions so Lua scripts can emit messages at
specific severity levels and query or change the active log level at
runtime without going through the `luna.system` namespace.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.log.debug(message)`

Emit a debug-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L31)*

---

#### `luna.log.error(message)`

Emit an error-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L73)*

---

#### `luna.log.getLevel()`

Return the name of the currently active minimum log level.

**Returns:** One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L127)*

---

#### `luna.log.info(message)`

Emit an info-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L45)*

---

#### `luna.log.print(level, message)`

Emit a log message from Lua at the specified severity level.

@param level : string @param message : string

Accepts the same level strings as `luna.log.setLevel`: `"debug"`, `"info"`, `"warn"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`. Unknown levels fall back to `info`.

**Parameters:**

- `level` — Severity level string.
- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L93)*

---

#### `luna.log.setLevel(level)`

Set the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.

@param level : string

**Parameters:**

- `level` — One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `luna.log.warn(message)`

Emit a warn-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L59)*

---


## luna.minimap

Lua API bindings for the `luna.minimap.*` minimap module.

Provides a `Minimap` UserData type with factory functions for creating
grid-based minimaps with terrain coloring, fog of war, tracked objects,
pings, markers, and viewport rectangle overlay.

*41 entries | 41 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.minimap.newMinimap(grid_w, grid_h, [display_w], [display_h])`

## luna.modding

Modding Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for modding api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

## luna.overlay

Lua API bindings for the `luna.overlay.*` screen-effect overlay module.

Registers the `luna.overlay` table and exposes a single factory:

- `luna.overlay.newOverlay(width?, height?)` — creates a `LuaOverlay`
  UserData object.

All overlay state lives entirely inside an `Rc<RefCell<Overlay>>`; the
`LuaOverlay` wrapper holds a clone of that smart pointer. Calling any
method borrows the `RefCell` for the duration of the call, then
releases it — the engine never holds a long-lived `borrow_mut` across
Lua callbacks.

The `register` function is called once during engine startup by the
`lua_api` module registration chain; it adds the `luna.overlay` table
to the root `luna` global.

*57 entries | 56 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.overlay.newOverlay([width], [height])`

*(undocumented)*

**Parameters:** `width`, `height`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L732)*

---

### Overlay Methods

#### `Overlay:clear()`

Resets all overlay subsystems to their inactive defaults.

Equivalent to calling `Overlay::clear()` — drops all live weather particles, deactivates flash/shake/fade/lightning, and disables ambient, clouds, fog, heat haze, vignette, and film grain. All parameters (intensity, colour, duration) are reset to their initial values. Useful when transitioning between scenes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L122)*

---

#### `Overlay:draw()`

Placeholder for draw — actual rendering handled by the game loop.

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L72)*

---

#### `Overlay:getAmbientColor()`

Returns the current ambient tint colour as `(r, g, b, a)`.

When time-of-day cycling is active the returned value may change every frame as `compute_color_from_time` advances. @return number, number, number, number

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L166)*

#### `Overlay:resize(w, h)`

Updates the internal canvas dimensions on window resize.

Informs the weather particle spawner of the new screen bounds so that particles are culled and spawned correctly after a window resize event. Does not drop existing particles. @param width : number @param height : number

#### `Overlay:setAmbientEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables automatic time-of-day ambient colour cycling.

When `true`, `update()` calls `compute_color_from_time()` each frame and overwrites `ambient.color`. When `false`, the colour set via `setAmbientColor` is used as a static tint. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L195)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudCount(count)`

Sets the number of cloud shadow blobs rendered each frame.

Higher counts produce denser, more uniform coverage. Each blob is positioned pseudo-randomly based on its index, so the layout is consistent across frames. @param count : number

**Parameters:** `count`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L439)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudOpacity(opacity)`

Sets the cloud shadow overlay opacity (0.0 = invisible, 1.0 = fully dark).

Controls how darkly the shadow blobs are blended over the scene. 0.3 gives a subtle day-time look; 0.7–0.9 simulates heavy overcast. @param opacity : number

**Parameters:** `opacity`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L487)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudScale(scale)`

Sets the relative size scale of each cloud shadow blob.

1.0 is the default blob size; smaller values produce compact dappled shadows; larger values produce wide overcast patches. @param scale : number

**Parameters:** `scale`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L471)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudShadows(enabled)`

Enables or disables the scrolling cloud shadow overlay.

Cloud shadows are rendered as soft blob-shaped shadow blobs drifting horizontally across the scene. Configure their appearance with `setCloudCount`, `setCloudScale`, and `setCloudOpacity`. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L422)*

---

#### `Overlay:setCloudSpeed(speed)`

Sets the horizontal scroll speed of cloud shadows in pixels per second.

The internal `offset` accumulator grows without bound; the renderer wraps it modulo screen width so shadows loop seamlessly. @param speed : number

**Parameters:** `speed`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L455)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFilmGrainEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables per-frame random film grain noise.

The noise pattern is regenerated every frame so it does not repeat or create a visible flicker texture. @param enabled : boolean

**Parameters:** `enabled`

*Source: [src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs](src/lua_api/overlay_api.rs#L644)*

---

#### `Overlay:setFilmGrainIntensity(intensity)`

Sets the film grain noise amplitude (0.0–1.0).

0.1–0.3 gives a subtle cinematic look. Values above 0.5 produce heavy grain that can obscure fine detail. @param intensity : number

#### `Overlay:setFogEnabled(enabled)`

Enables or disables atmospheric fog.

@param enabled : boolean Enables or disables the atmospheric fog overlay.

When enabled, a translucent colour rectangle is blended over the full scene every frame. Configure thickness via `setFogDensity` and colour via `setFogColor`.
